        
Business Layer Human Resources Information
-------------------------------------------------
        
General Information
-------------------------------------------------
Modified : Fri Sep 29 10:17:09 CDT 2017
        
Name : Human Resources Information
Description : Human Resource Information universe provides information about HR activities that happen daily at USAA.In addition to the daily activities , the universe provides Exit Interview information too.
        
Data Foundation : Human Resources Information
        
            
    Statistics
    -------------------------------------------------
        Folders : 116
        Business Layer Views : 2
        Dimensions : 1087
        Attributes : 0
        Measures : 260
        Filters : 44
        Queries : 0
        Lists of Values : 7
        Parameters : 0
        Navigation Paths : 6
            
    Properties
    -------------------------------------------------
        Allow use of subqueries : True
        Allow use of union, intersect, and minus operators : True
        Multiple SQL statements for each measure : False
        Allow complex operands in Query Panel : True
        Limit size of result set to : 5000000 Rows
        Limit execution time to : 15 minutes

    Dimension: Day Sid
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Day Sid
    state : Hidden
    dataType : Numeric
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.DAY_SID
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    Dimension: Business Processed Month Descrtiption (MM - Month)
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Business Processed Month Descrtiption (MM - Month)
    description : The month on which a record is processed in 'MM-Month' format.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : (substr(A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_NUM,5,2)) ||'-'|| A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_DESCR
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort
            
    Dimension: Custom Business Processed Month Descrtiption (MM - Month)
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Custom Business Processed Month Descrtiption (MM - Month)
    description : The month on which a record is processed in 'MM' format.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : Case When to_char(date_trunc('Month',CURRENT_DATE)-1,'MM')=A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_YR_NUM THEN 'Current Month'
Else (substr(A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_NUM,5,2)) ||'-'|| A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_DESCR  END 
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    Dimension: Custom Business Processed Year Number (YYYY)
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Custom Business Processed Year Number (YYYY)
    description : The Year on which a record is processed.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : Case when Year(date_trunc('Month',CURRENT_DATE)-1)=A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.YEAR_NUM THEN 'Current Year'
Else to_char(A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.YEAR_NUM,'9999')  END
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    Dimension: Location Short Name
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Location Short Name
    description : Abbreviated name for a location used for reporting purposes.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : CASE 
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Tampa Campus%'   Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Tampa ','') ||' ('||A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Phoenix Campus%'   Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Phoenix ','') ||' ('||A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Colorado Springs Campus%'   Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Colorado Springs ','') ||' ('||A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'

WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%University%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'University','UNV.')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%San Antonio%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'San Antonio ','')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Phoenix%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Phoenix ','')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Colorado Springs%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Colorado Springs ','')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Tampa%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Tampa ','')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Bank Complex%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Bank Complex','Bank')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Chesapeake%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Chesapeake','CPK')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Two Addison Circle%' Then replace(A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Two Addison Circle WMC','Two ADS Circle')  
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Off-Site%'   Then A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM||' ('||A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
ELSE A_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM END
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    Dimension: Location Rollup Name
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Location Rollup Name
    description : Description for the location rollup code that groups business sites into Major location footprints, i.e. San Antonio, DFW, etc. This is used for reporting purposes
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : CASE 
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='OTH' Then 'Other'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='TFL' Then 'Tampa'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='SAT' Then 'San Antonio'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='DFW' Then 'Dallas-Fort Worth'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='PHX' Then 'Phoenix'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='COL' Then 'Colorado Springs'
WHEN A_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='VBN' Then 'Virginia Beach-Norfolk'
Else 'Unknown' End

    Dimension: Prior Location Short Name
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Prior Location Short Name
    description : Abbreviated name for a location used for reporting purposes.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : CASE 
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Tampa Campus%'   Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Tampa ','') ||' ('||A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Phoenix Campus%'   Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Phoenix ','') ||' ('||A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Colorado Springs Campus%'   Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Colorado Springs ','') ||' ('||A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'

WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%University%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'University','UNV.')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%San Antonio%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'San Antonio ','')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Phoenix%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Phoenix ','')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Colorado Springs%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Colorado Springs ','')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Tampa%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Tampa ','')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Bank Complex%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Bank Complex','Bank')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Chesapeake%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Chesapeake','CPK')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Two Addison Circle%' Then replace(A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM,'Two Addison Circle WMC','Two ADS Circle')  
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM LIKE '%Off-Site%'   Then A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM||' ('||A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD||')'
ELSE A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_NM END
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    description : Description for the location rollup code that groups business sites into Major location footprints, i.e. San Antonio, DFW, etc. This is used for reporting purposes
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : CASE 
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='OTH' Then 'Other'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='TFL' Then 'Tampa'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='SAT' Then 'San Antonio'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='DFW' Then 'Dallas-Fort Worth'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='PHX' Then 'Phoenix'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='COL' Then 'Colorado Springs'
WHEN A_PRIOR_LOCATION.LOCATION_ROLLUP_CD='VBN' Then 'Virginia Beach-Norfolk'
Else 'Unknown' End

A_WORKER_PROFILE.ETHNICITY_SHORT_NM ='!'
 Then 'Not Specified' Else A_WORKER_PROFILE.ETHNICITY_SHORT_NM  end 
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    SQL Definition : Case When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='Y' Then 'Other Family'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='Y' Then 'Veteran'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='N' Then 'Veteran'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='N' Then 'None'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='N' Then 'Spouse/Domestic Partner'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='Y' Then 'Veteran'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='N' Then 'Veteran'
When A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SELF_IND='N' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_SPOUSE_IND='Y' and A_WORKER_PROFILE.MILITARY_AFFIL_OTHER_IND='Y' Then 'Spouse/Domestic Partner'
Else 'Unknown' End

    Dimension: Worker Performance Rating Short Code
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Worker Performance Rating Short Code
    description : Abbreviated name for a worker performance rating used for reporting purposes.

    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : CASE
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) ='!' Then 'None'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) ='N' Then 'None'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =0 Then 'None'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =1 Then 'NR'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =2 Then 'BE'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =3 Then 'PME'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =4 Then 'ME'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =5 Then 'EE'
WHEN SUBSTR(A_WORKER_PROFILE.PERFORMANCE_RATING_CD,1,1) =6 Then 'FE' Else 'NR' END
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

    Dimension: Job Title Rollup Name
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Job Title Rollup Name
    description : Job title rollup is created specifically for D&A report.
    state : Active
    dataType : String
    access : Public
    forResult : true
    SQL Definition : case when instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,',',-1,1) > 0 and instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,'(inactive)',1,1) > 0 then substr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,1, instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' (inactive)',-1,1))
when instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,',',-1,1) > 0 then A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM
when instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,'- NX',-1,1) > 0 then trim(substr(substr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,1,instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' - NX',-1,1)),1,instr(rtrim(substr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,1,instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' - NX',-1,1)),' '),' ',-1,1)))
when instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,'(inactive)',-1,1) > 0 then trim(substr(substr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,1,instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' (inactive)',-1,1)),1,instr(rtrim(substr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,1,instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' (inactive)',-1,1)),' '),' ',-1,1)))
else trim(substr(rtrim(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,'(inactive)'),1,instr(A_JOB_PROFILE.JOB_TITLE_NM,' ',-1,1))) END
    Can be used in  : Result, Filter, Sort

Filters
-------------------------------------------------
        
Filter: Filter Headcount Greater Than Zero
-------------------------------------------------
coreItemIdentifier : 
overridableProperties : -1
businessName : Filter Headcount Greater Than Zero
description : Filters headcounts from headcount that has headcount measure greater than zero
state : Active
filterType : Native
compulsory : false
filterScope : Universe
applyOnListOfValues : false
Where expression : @Aggregate_Aware(A_CUR_FC_HC.HEAD_CNT,A_FC_HC.HEAD_CNT)>0
        
Filter: Filter Sum of All Measures Greater Than Zero
-------------------------------------------------
coreItemIdentifier : 
overridableProperties : -1
businessName : Filter Sum of All Measures Greater Than Zero
description : Filter that retrieve only rows that has sum of all measures greater than zero.
state : Active
filterType : Native
compulsory : false
filterScope : Universe
applyOnListOfValues : false
Where expression : (A_CUR_ACTIVITY_AGG.HIRE_CNT+
A_CUR_ACTIVITY_AGG.INTERNAL_HIRE_CNT+
A_CUR_ACTIVITY_AGG.REHIRE_CNT+
A_CUR_ACTIVITY_AGG.VOLUNTARY_SEPARATION_CNT+
A_CUR_ACTIVITY_AGG.INVOLUNTARY_SEPARATION_CNT+

List of Values
-------------------------------------------------
            
    SQL List of Values: Cost Center L4 Name
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : Cost Center L4 Name
    hidden : false
    allowEdit : false
    automaticRefresh : false
    hierarchical : false
    query : SELECT * FROM (
SELECT ' All Cost Center L4s' AS "Cost Center L4 Name"
FROM ADMIN.M_CWF_DM_COR_COST_CENTER
UNION
SELECT DISTINCT COST_CENTER_L4_NM
FROM ADMIN.M_CWF_DM_COR_COST_CENTER
) A
ORDER BY 1

    SQL List of Values: LOV For Current Year and Previous 2 Year
    -------------------------------------------------
    coreItemIdentifier : 
    overridableProperties : -1
    businessName : LOV For Current Year and Previous 2 Year
    hidden : false
    allowEdit : false
    automaticRefresh : false
    hierarchical : false
    query : SELECT
DISTINCT   A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.MONTH_NUM
FROM
  PHRAEDB.ADMIN.M_CWF_DM_DAY  A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY 
  INNER JOIN PHRAELB.ADMIN.M_CWF_LK_AS_OF_DATE  A_LK_ASOFDATE_ACT ON (A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.DAY_DT<=A_LK_ASOFDATE_ACT.AS_OF_DT)
  WHERE
  ( A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.DAY_DT >= add_months(date_trunc('YEAR',( A_LK_ASOFDATE_ACT.UA_WF_LST_LOAD_DT  ) ),-24)
AND 
A_BUSINESS_PROCESS_DAY.DAY_DT <= ( A_LK_ASOFDATE_ACT.AS_OF_DT )  )

Navigation Paths
-------------------------------------------------
            
    Navigation Path: Cost Center
    -------------------------------------------------
    Job Title Rollup Name : Job Profile\Job Profile\Job Title Rollup Name
            Job title rollup is created specifically for D&A report.
    Cost Center L4 Name : Cost Center\Cost Center\Cost Center L4 Name
            The company staff agency (COSA) of a cost center.

    Cost Center L8 Name : Cost Center\Cost Center\Cost Center L8 Name
            The direct report of a cost center.

    Cost Center L11 Name : Cost Center\Cost Center\Cost Center L11 Name
            The functional area of a cost center.

    Cost Center L12 Name : Cost Center\Cost Center\Cost Center L12 Name
            The business group of a cost center.

            
    Navigation Path: Business Processed Time
    -------------------------------------------------
    Business Processed Year Number (YYYY) : Business Processing Dates\Business Processed Year Number (YYYY)
            The Year on which a record is processed.
    Business Processed Month Number YYYYMM : Business Processing Dates\Business Processed Month Number YYYYMM
            The month on which a record is processed in 'YYYYMM' format.
    Business Processed Day Description (YYYY-MM-DD) : Business Processing Dates\Business Processed Day Description (YYYY-MM-DD)
            The day on which a record is processed in YYYY-MM-DD format.
